  syntax {Sort} Sort ::= Sort "#Or" Sort [assoc, comm, format(%i%1%d%n%2%n%i%3%d), group(mlOp), left, mlOp, symbol(#Or), unit(#Bottom)]
  syntax {Sort} Sort ::= Sort "#Implies" Sort [format(%i%1%d%n%2%n%i%3%d), group(mlImplies, mlOp), mlOp, symbol(#Implies)]
